local runDummyScript = function(f,scri)
local oldenv = getfenv(f)
local newenv = setmetatable({}, {
__index = function(_, k)
if k:lower() == 'script' then
return scri
else
return oldenv[k]
end
end
})
setfenv(f, newenv)
ypcall(function() f() end)
end

		object.Transparency = 1

if value1 < 29.8 then

if Animate.Value == "none" then
		Animate.Value = "Walk"
end

else

if value1 < 100 then value1 = value1+1 end

if Animate.Value == "none" then
		Animate.Value = "Run"
end

end

script.Parent.BodyVelocity.velocity = script.Parent.CFrame.lookVector*value1
end
if script.Parent.Throttle == 0 or script.Parent.Throttle == -1 then

if value1 > 0 then
if value1 < 30 then

value1 = value1 - .4

if Animate.Value == "none" then
		Animate.Value = "Walk"
end

else

if value1 < 101 then value1 = value1-2 end

if Animate.Value == "none" then
		Animate.Value = "Run"
end
end

else
		value1 = 0
end

script.Parent.BodyVelocity.velocity = script.Parent.CFrame.lookVector*value1
end

if script.Parent.Steer == 1 then

if Animate.Value == "none" then
		Animate.Value = "RTurn"
end

script.Parent.BodyGyro.cframe = script.Parent.BodyGyro.cframe * CFrame.fromEulerAnglesXYZ(0,-.02,0)
end

if Animate.Value == "none" then
		Animate.Value = "LTurn"
end

end

walk = 0

function Animate()
	if animating then return end
	animating = true

	if animate.Value == "Walk" then

	script.Parent.BodyVelocity.maxForce = Vector3.new(4e11, 4e3, 4e11)

	if walk == 0 then
	for i = 1, 10 do
	RShoulder.C1 = RShoulder.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.pi/3/10)
	RElbow.C1 = RElbow.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, -math.pi/2/10)
	RFAnkle.C1 = RFAnkle.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, -math.pi/3/10)
	LShoulder.C1 = LShoulder.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, -math.pi/16/10)
	LFAnkle.C1 = LFAnkle.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.pi/8/10)

	RHip.C1 = RHip.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, -math.pi/6/10)
	RKnee.C1 = RKnee.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.pi/8/10)
	LHip.C1 = LHip.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.pi/16/10)
	LKnee.C1 = LKnee.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.pi/4/10)
	LBAnkle.C1 = LBAnkle.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, -math.pi/3/10)

	Neck.C1 = Neck.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, -math.pi/24/10)
	Waist.C1 = Waist.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, -math.pi/24/10, 0)
	Saddle.C1 = Saddle.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, -math.pi/48/10, 0)
	wait()
	end

	for i = 1, 10 do
	RShoulder.C1 = RShoulder.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, -math.pi*2/9/10)
	RElbow.C1 = RElbow.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.pi/2/10)
	RFAnkle.C1 = RFAnkle.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.pi/3/10)
	LFAnkle.C1 = LFAnkle.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, -math.pi/6/10)

	Neck.C1 = Neck.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.pi/12/10)
	wait()

	Saddle.C1 = Saddle.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, math.pi/48/10, 0)

	wait()
	end

	walk = 1

	else

	for i = 1, 10 do
	LShoulder.C1 = LShoulder.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.pi/3/10)
	LElbow.C1 = LElbow.C1 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, -math.pi/2/10)
